There are multiple approaches to defining custom tools in Strands, with differences between Python and TypeScript implementations.

<starlight-tab-item data-label="Python"> &lt;p&gt;Python supports three approaches to defining tools:&lt;/p&gt;&lt;ul&gt; &lt;li&gt; &lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Python functions with the &lt;a href=&quot;/docs/api/python/strands.tools.decorator/#tool&quot;&gt;&amp;lt;code dir=&amp;quot;auto&amp;quot;&amp;gt;@tool&amp;lt;/code&amp;gt;&lt;/a&gt; decorator&lt;/strong&gt;: Transform regular Python functions into tools by adding a simple decorator. This approach leverages Python’s docstrings and type hints to automatically generate tool specifications.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;/li&gt; &lt;li&gt; &lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Class-based tools with the &lt;a href=&quot;/docs/api/python/strands.tools.decorator/#tool&quot;&gt;&amp;lt;code dir=&amp;quot;auto&amp;quot;&amp;gt;@tool&amp;lt;/code&amp;gt;&lt;/a&gt; decorator&lt;/strong&gt;: Create tools within classes to maintain state and leverage object-oriented programming patterns.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;/li&gt; &lt;li&gt; &lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Python modules following a specific format&lt;/strong&gt;: Define tools by creating Python modules that contain a tool specification and a matching function. This approach gives you more control over the tool’s definition and is useful for dependency-free implementations of tools.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;/li&gt; &lt;/ul&gt; </starlight-tab-item><starlight-tab-item data-label="TypeScript"> &lt;p&gt;TypeScript supports two main approaches:&lt;/p&gt;&lt;ul&gt; &lt;li&gt; &lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;tool() function with &lt;a href=&quot;https://zod.dev/&quot;&gt;Zod&lt;/a&gt; or JSON schemas&lt;/strong&gt;: Create tools using the &lt;code dir=&quot;auto&quot;&gt;tool()&lt;/code&gt; function with either Zod schemas for type-safe validated input, or plain JSON Schema objects for schema-only definitions without runtime validation.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;/li&gt; &lt;li&gt; &lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Class-based tools extending FunctionTool&lt;/strong&gt;: Create tools within classes to maintain shared state and resources.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;/li&gt; &lt;/ul&gt; </starlight-tab-item>

## Tool Creation Examples

### Basic Example

<starlight-tab-item data-label="Python"> &lt;p&gt;Here’s a simple example of a function decorated as a tool:&lt;/p&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;expressive-code&quot;&gt;&lt;link rel=&quot;stylesheet&quot; href=&quot;/\_astro/ec.lgrc4.css&quot;/&gt;&lt;script type=&quot;module&quot; src=&quot;/\_astro/ec.0vx5m.js&quot;&gt;&lt;/script&gt;&lt;figure class=&quot;frame&quot;&gt;&lt;figcaption class=&quot;header&quot;&gt;&lt;/figcaption&gt;&lt;pre data-language=&quot;python&quot; dir=&quot;ltr&quot;&gt;&lt;code&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;ec-line&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;code&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#BF3441;--1:#F97583&quot;&gt;from&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#24292E;--1:#E1E4E8&quot;&gt; strands &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#BF3441;--1:#F97583&quot;&gt;import&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#24292E;--1:#E1E4E8&quot;&gt; tool&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;ec-line&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;code&quot;&gt; &lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;ec-line&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;code&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#6F42C1;--1:#B392F0&quot;&gt;@tool&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;ec-line&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;code&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#BF3441;--1:#F97583&quot;&gt;def&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#24292E;--1:#E1E4E8&quot;&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#6F42C1;--1:#B392F0&quot;&gt;weather\_forecast&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#24292E;--1:#E1E4E8&quot;&gt;(city: &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#005CC5;--1:#79B8FF&quot;&gt;str&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#24292E;--1:#E1E4E8&quot;&gt;, days: &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#005CC5;--1:#79B8FF&quot;&gt;int&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#24292E;--1:#E1E4E8&quot;&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#BF3441;--1:#F97583&quot;&gt;=&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#24292E;--1:#E1E4E8&quot;&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#005CC5;--1:#79B8FF&quot;&gt;3&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#24292E;--1:#E1E4E8&quot;&gt;) -&amp;gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#005CC5;--1:#79B8FF&quot;&gt;str&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#24292E;--1:#E1E4E8&quot;&gt;:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;ec-line&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;code&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;indent&quot;&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#032F62;--1:#9ECBFF&quot;&gt;&amp;quot;&amp;quot;&amp;quot;Get weather forecast for a city.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;ec-line&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;code&quot;&gt; &lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;ec-line&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;code&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;indent&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#032F62;--1:#9ECBFF&quot;&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#032F62;--1:#9ECBFF&quot;&gt;Args:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;ec-line&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;code&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;indent&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#032F62;--1:#9ECBFF&quot;&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#032F62;--1:#9ECBFF&quot;&gt;city: The name of the city&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;ec-line&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;code&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;indent&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#032F62;--1:#9ECBFF&quot;&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#032F62;--1:#9ECBFF&quot;&gt;days: Number of days for the forecast&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;ec-line&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;code&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;indent&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#032F62;--1:#9ECBFF&quot;&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#032F62;--1:#9ECBFF&quot;&gt;&amp;quot;&amp;quot;&amp;quot;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;ec-line&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;code&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;indent&quot;&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#BF3441;--1:#F97583&quot;&gt;return&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#24292E;--1:#E1E4E8&quot;&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#BF3441;--1:#F97583&quot;&gt;f&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#032F62;--1:#9ECBFF&quot;&gt;&amp;quot;Weather forecast for &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#005CC5;--1:#79B8FF&quot;&gt;{&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#24292E;--1:#E1E4E8&quot;&gt;city&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#005CC5;--1:#79B8FF&quot;&gt;}&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#032F62;--1:#9ECBFF&quot;&gt; for the next &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#005CC5;--1:#79B8FF&quot;&gt;{&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#24292E;--1:#E1E4E8&quot;&gt;days&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#005CC5;--1:#79B8FF&quot;&gt;}&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#032F62;--1:#9ECBFF&quot;&gt; days...&amp;quot;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/code&gt;&lt;/pre&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;copy&quot;&gt;&lt;div aria-live=&quot;polite&quot;&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;button title=&quot;Copy to clipboard&quot; data-copied=&quot;Copied!&quot; data-code=&quot;from strands import tool@tooldef weather\_forecast(city: str, days: int = 3) -&gt; str: &amp;#34;&amp;#34;&amp;#34;Get weather forecast for a city. Args: city: The name of the city days: Number of days for the forecast &amp;#34;&amp;#34;&amp;#34; return f&amp;#34;Weather forecast for {city} for the next {days} days...&amp;#34;&quot;&gt;&lt;div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/button&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/figure&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;p&gt;The decorator extracts information from your function’s docstring to create the tool specification. The first paragraph becomes the tool’s description, and the “Args” section provides parameter descriptions. These are combined with the function’s type hints to create a complete tool specification.&lt;/p&gt; </starlight-tab-item><starlight-tab-item data-label="TypeScript"> &lt;p&gt;Here’s a simple example of a function based tool with Zod:&lt;/p&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;expressive-code&quot;&gt;&lt;figure class=&quot;frame&quot;&gt;&lt;figcaption class=&quot;header&quot;&gt;&lt;/figcaption&gt;&lt;pre data-language=&quot;typescript&quot; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#005CC5;--1:#79B8FF&quot;&gt;weatherTool&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#24292E;--1:#E1E4E8&quot;&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#BF3441;--1:#F97583&quot;&gt;=&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#24292E;--1:#E1E4E8&quot;&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#6F42C1;--1:#B392F0&quot;&gt;tool&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#24292E;--1:#E1E4E8&quot;&gt;({&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;ec-line&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;code&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;indent&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#24292E;--1:#E1E4E8&quot;&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#24292E;--1:#E1E4E8&quot;&gt;name: &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#032F62;--1:#9ECBFF&quot;&gt;&amp;#39;weather\_forecast&amp;#39;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#24292E;--1:#E1E4E8&quot;&gt;,&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;ec-line&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;code&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;indent&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#24292E;--1:#E1E4E8&quot;&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#032F62;--1:#9ECBFF&quot;&gt;\`Weather forecast for ${&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#24292E;--1:#E1E4E8&quot;&gt;input&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#032F62;--1:#9ECBFF&quot;&gt;.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#24292E;--1:#E1E4E8&quot;&gt;city&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#032F62;--1:#9ECBFF&quot;&gt;} for the next ${&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#24292E;--1:#E1E4E8&quot;&gt;input&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#032F62;--1:#9ECBFF&quot;&gt;.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#24292E;--1:#E1E4E8&quot;&gt;days&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#032F62;--1:#9ECBFF&quot;&gt;} days...\`&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;ec-line&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;code&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;indent&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#24292E;--1:#E1E4E8&quot;&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#24292E;--1:#E1E4E8&quot;&gt;},&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;ec-line&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;code&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#24292E;--1:#E1E4E8&quot;&gt;})&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/code&gt;&lt;/pre&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;copy&quot;&gt;&lt;div aria-live=&quot;polite&quot;&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;button title=&quot;Copy to clipboard&quot; data-copied=&quot;Copied!&quot; data-code=&quot;const weatherTool = tool({ name: &#39;weather\_forecast&#39;, description: &#39;Get weather forecast for a city&#39;, inputSchema: z.object({ city: z.string().describe(&#39;The name of the city&#39;), days: z.number().default(3).describe(&#39;Number of days for the forecast&#39;), }), callback: (input) =&gt; { return \`Weather forecast for ${input.city} for the next ${input.days} days...\` },})&quot;&gt;&lt;div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/button&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/figure&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;p&gt;The &lt;code dir=&quot;auto&quot;&gt;tool()&lt;/code&gt; function accepts either a &lt;a href=&quot;https://zod.dev/&quot;&gt;Zod&lt;/a&gt; schema or a plain JSON Schema object as &lt;code dir=&quot;auto&quot;&gt;inputSchema&lt;/code&gt;. With Zod, input is validated at runtime and the callback receives typed input. With JSON Schema, the schema is passed through as-is and the callback receives &lt;code dir=&quot;auto&quot;&gt;unknown&lt;/code&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Here’s the same tool using a JSON Schema object instead:&lt;/p&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;expressive-code&quot;&gt;&lt;figure class=&quot;frame&quot;&gt;&lt;figcaption class=&quot;header&quot;&gt;&lt;/figcaption&gt;&lt;pre data-language=&quot;typescript&quot; dir=&quot;ltr&quot;&gt;&lt;code&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;ec-line&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;code&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#BF3441;--1:#F97583&quot;&gt;const&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#24292E;--1:#E1E4E8&quot;&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#005CC5;--1:#79B8FF&quot;&gt;weatherTool&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#24292E;--1:#E1E4E8&quot;&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#BF3441;--1:#F97583&quot;&gt;=&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#24292E;--1:#E1E4E8&quot;&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#6F42C1;--1:#B392F0&quot;&gt;tool&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#24292E;--1:#E1E4E8&quot;&gt;({&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;ec-line&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;code&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;indent&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#24292E;--1:#E1E4E8&quot;&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#24292E;--1:#E1E4E8&quot;&gt;name: &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#032F62;--1:#9ECBFF&quot;&gt;&amp;#39;weather\_forecast&amp;#39;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#24292E;--1:#E1E4E8&quot;&gt;,&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;ec-line&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;code&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;indent&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#24292E;--1:#E1E4E8&quot;&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#24292E;--1:#E1E4E8&quot;&gt;description: &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#032F62;--1:#9ECBFF&quot;&gt;&amp;#39;Get weather forecast for a city&amp;#39;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#24292E;--1:#E1E4E8&quot;&gt;,&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;ec-line&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;code&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;indent&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#24292E;--1:#E1E4E8&quot;&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#24292E;--1:#E1E4E8&quot;&gt;inputSchema: {&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;ec-line&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;code&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;indent&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#24292E;--1:#E1E4E8&quot;&gt; data-copied=&quot;Copied!&quot; data-code=&quot;const weatherTool = tool({ name: &#39;get\_weather&#39;, description: &#39;Retrieves weather forecast for a specified location&#39;, inputSchema: z.object({ city: z.string().describe(&#39;The name of the city&#39;), days: z.number().default(3).describe(&#39;Number of days for the forecast&#39;), }), callback: (input: { city: any; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#BF3441;--1:#F97583&quot;&gt;return&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#24292E;--1:#E1E4E8&quot;&gt; width &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#BF3441;--1:#F97583&quot;&gt;\*&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#24292E;--1:#E1E4E8&quot;&gt; height&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;ec-line&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;code&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;indent&quot;&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#BF3441;--1:#F97583&quot;&gt;return&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#24292E;--1:#E1E4E8&quot;&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#005CC5;--1:#79B8FF&quot;&gt;0.0&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/code&gt;&lt;/pre&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;copy&quot;&gt;&lt;div aria-live=&quot;polite&quot;&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;button title=&quot;Copy to clipboard&quot; data-copied=&quot;Copied!&quot; data-code=&quot;@tool( inputSchema={ &amp;#34;json&amp;#34;: { &amp;#34;type&amp;#34;: &amp;#34;object&amp;#34;, &amp;#34;properties&amp;#34;: { &amp;#34;shape&amp;#34;: { &amp;#34;type&amp;#34;: &amp;#34;string&amp;#34;, &amp;#34;enum&amp;#34;: \[&amp;#34;circle&amp;#34;, &amp;#34;rectangle&amp;#34;\], &amp;#34;description&amp;#34;: &amp;#34;The shape type&amp;#34; }, &amp;#34;radius&amp;#34;: {&amp;#34;type&amp;#34;: &amp;#34;number&amp;#34;, &amp;#34;description&amp;#34;: &amp;#34;Radius for circle&amp;#34;}, &amp;#34;width&amp;#34;: {&amp;#34;type&amp;#34;: &amp;#34;number&amp;#34;, &amp;#34;description&amp;#34;: &amp;#34;Width for rectangle&amp;#34;}, &amp;#34;height&amp;#34;: {&amp;#34;type&amp;#34;: &amp;#34;number&amp;#34;, &amp;#34;description&amp;#34;: &amp;#34;Height for rectangle&amp;#34;} }, &amp;#34;required&amp;#34;: \[&amp;#34;shape&amp;#34;\] } })def calculate\_area(shape: str, radius: float = None, width: float = None, height: float = None) -&gt; float: &amp;#34;&amp;#34;&amp;#34;Calculate area of a shape.&amp;#34;&amp;#34;&amp;#34; if shape == &amp;#34;circle&amp;#34;: return 3.14159 \* radius \*\* 2 elif shape == &amp;#34;rectangle&amp;#34;: return width \* height return 0.0&quot;&gt;&lt;div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/button&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/figure&gt;&lt;/div&gt; </starlight-tab-item><starlight-tab-item data-label="TypeScript"> &lt;p&gt;In TypeScript, &lt;code dir=&quot;auto&quot;&gt;inputSchema&lt;/code&gt; is always provided explicitly in the &lt;code dir=&quot;auto&quot;&gt;tool()&lt;/code&gt; configuration - as either a Zod schema or a JSON Schema object. See the &lt;a href=&quot;#basic-example&quot;&gt;basic example&lt;/a&gt; above for both approaches.&lt;/p&gt; </starlight-tab-item>

## Using and Customizing Tools:

### Loading Function-Based Tools

To use function-based tools, simply pass them to the agent:

<starlight-tab-item data-label="Python"> &lt;div class=&quot;expressive-code&quot;&gt;&lt;figure class=&quot;frame&quot;&gt;&lt;figcaption class=&quot;header&quot;&gt;&lt;/figcaption&gt;&lt;pre data-language=&quot;python&quot; ### Custom Return Type

</starlight-tab-item><starlight-tab-item data-label="TypeScript"> &lt;p&gt;In Typescript, your tool’s return value is automatically converted into a &lt;code dir=&quot;auto&quot;&gt;ToolResultBlock&lt;/code&gt;. You can return &lt;strong&gt;any&lt;/strong&gt; JSON serializable object:&lt;/p&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;expressive-code&quot;&gt;&lt;figure class=&quot;frame&quot;&gt;&lt;figcaption class=&quot;header&quot;&gt;&lt;/figcaption&gt;&lt;pre data-language=&quot;typescript&quot; dir=&quot;ltr&quot;&gt;&lt;code&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;ec-line&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;code&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#BF3441;--1:#F97583&quot;&gt;const&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#24292E;--1:#E1E4E8&quot;&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#005CC5;--1:#79B8FF&quot;&gt;weatherTool&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#24292E;--1:#E1E4E8&quot;&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#BF3441;--1:#F97583&quot;&gt;=&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#24292E;--1:#E1E4E8&quot;&gt; For more details, see the [Tool Response Format](#tool-response-format) section below.

### Async Invocation

Function tools may also be defined async. Strands will invoke all async tools concurrently.

&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#BF3441;--1:#F97583&quot;&gt;return&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#24292E;--1:#E1E4E8&quot;&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#032F62;--1:#9ECBFF&quot;&gt;\`Inserted data into ${&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#24292E;--1:#E1E4E8&quot;&gt;input&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#032F62;--1:#9ECBFF&quot;&gt;.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#24292E;--1:#E1E4E8&quot;&gt;table&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#032F62;--1:#9ECBFF&quot;&gt;}: ${&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#005CC5;--1:#79B8FF&quot;&gt;JSON&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#032F62;--1:#9ECBFF&quot;&gt;.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#6F42C1;--1:#B392F0&quot;&gt;stringify&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#032F62;--1:#9ECBFF&quot;&gt;(&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#24292E;--1:#E1E4E8&quot;&gt;input&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#032F62;--1:#9ECBFF&quot;&gt;.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#24292E;--1:#E1E4E8&quot;&gt;data&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#032F62;--1:#9ECBFF&quot;&gt;)&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#032F62;--1:#9ECBFF&quot;&gt;}\`&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;ec-line&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;code&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;indent&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#24292E;--1:#E1E4E8&quot;&gt; data-copied=&quot;Copied!&quot; data-code=&quot;const insertDataTool = tool({ name: &#39;insert\_data&#39;, description: &#39;Insert data with progress updates&#39;, inputSchema: z.object({ table: z.string().describe(&#39;The table name&#39;), data: z.record(z.string(), z.any()).describe(&#39;The data to insert&#39;), }), callback: async function\* (input: { table: string data: Record&lt;string, any&gt; }): AsyncGenerator&lt;string, string, unknown&gt; { yield &#39;Starting data insertion...&#39; await new Promise((resolve) =&gt; setTimeout(resolve, 1000)) yield &#39;Validating data...&#39; await new Promise((resolve) =&gt; setTimeout(resolve, 1000)) return \`Inserted data into ${input.table}: ${JSON.stringify(input.data)}\` },})&quot;&gt;&lt;div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/button&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/figure&gt;&lt;/div&gt; </starlight-tab-item>

### ToolContext

Tools can access their execution context to interact with the invoking agent, current tool use data, and invocation state. The [<code dir="auto">ToolContext</code>](/docs/api/python/strands.types.tools#ToolContext) provides this access:

<starlight-tab-item data-label="Python"> &lt;p&gt;In Python, set &lt;code dir=&quot;auto&quot;&gt;context=True&lt;/code&gt; in the decorator and include a &lt;code dir=&quot;auto&quot;&gt;tool\_context&lt;/code&gt; #### Accessing State in Tools

<starlight-tab-item data-label="Python"> &lt;p&gt;The &lt;code dir=&quot;auto&quot;&gt;invocation\_state&lt;/code&gt; attribute in &lt;code dir=&quot;auto&quot;&gt;ToolContext&lt;/code&gt; provides access to data passed through the agent invocation. This is particularly useful for:&lt;/p&gt;&lt;ol&gt; &lt;li&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Request Context&lt;/strong&gt;: Access session IDs, user information, or request-specific data&lt;/li&gt; &lt;li&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Multi-Agent Shared State&lt;/strong&gt;: In &lt;a href=&quot;/docs/user-guide/concepts/multi-agent/graph/&quot;&gt;Graph&lt;/a&gt; and &lt;a href=&quot;/docs/user-guide/concepts/multi-agent/swarm/&quot;&gt;Swarm&lt;/a&gt; patterns, access state shared across all agents&lt;/li&gt; &lt;li&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Per-Invocation Overrides&lt;/strong&gt;: Override behavior or settings for specific requests&lt;/li&gt; data-copied=&quot;Copied!&quot; data-code=&quot;from strands import tool, Agent, ToolContextimport requests@tool(context=True)def api\_call(query: str, tool\_context: ToolContext) -&gt; dict: &amp;#34;&amp;#34;&amp;#34;Make an API call with user context. Args: query: The search query to send to the API tool\_context: Context containing user information &amp;#34;&amp;#34;&amp;#34; user\_id = tool\_context.invocation\_state.get(&amp;#34;user\_id&amp;#34;) response = requests.get( &amp;#34;https://api.example.com/search&amp;#34;, headers={&amp;#34;X-User-ID&amp;#34;: user\_id}, params={&amp;#34;q&amp;#34;: query} ) return response.json()agent = Agent(tools=\[api\_call\])result = agent(&amp;#34;Get my profile data&amp;#34;, user\_id=&amp;#34;user123&amp;#34;)&quot;&gt;&lt;div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/button&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/figure&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Invocation State Compared To Other Approaches&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;It’s important to understand how invocation state compares to other approaches that impact tool execution:&lt;/p&gt;&lt;ul&gt; &lt;li&gt; &lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Tool Parameters&lt;/strong&gt;: Use for data that the LLM should reason about and provide based on the user’s request. Examples include search queries, file paths, calculation inputs, or any data the agent needs to determine from context.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;/li&gt; &lt;li&gt; &lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Invocation State&lt;/strong&gt;: Use for context and configuration that should not appear in prompts but affects tool behavior. Best suited for parameters that can change between agent invocations. Examples include user IDs for personalization, session IDs, or user flags.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;/li&gt; &lt;li&gt; &lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;#class-based-tools&quot;&gt;Class-based tools&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;: Use for configuration that doesn’t change between requests and requires initialization. Examples include API keys, database connection strings, service endpoints, or shared resources that need setup.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;/li&gt; &lt;/ul&gt; </starlight-tab-item><starlight-tab-item data-label="TypeScript"> &lt;p&gt;In TypeScript, tools access &lt;strong&gt;agent state&lt;/strong&gt; through &lt;code dir=&quot;auto&quot;&gt;context.agent.appState&lt;/code&gt;. The state provides key-value storage that persists across tool invocations but is not passed to the model:&lt;/p&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;expressive-code&quot;&gt;&lt;figure class=&quot;frame&quot;&gt;&lt;figcaption class=&quot;header&quot;&gt;&lt;/figcaption&gt;&lt;pre data-language=&quot;typescript&quot; &lt;li&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Request Context&lt;/strong&gt;: Access session IDs, user information, or request-specific data&lt;/li&gt; &lt;li&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Multi-Agent Shared State&lt;/strong&gt;: In multi-agent patterns, access state shared across all agents&lt;/li&gt; ### Tool Streaming

<starlight-tab-item data-label="Python"> &lt;p&gt;Async tools can yield intermediate results to provide real-time progress updates. ## Class-Based Tools

Class-based tools allow you to create tools that maintain state and leverage object-oriented programming patterns. This approach is useful when your tools need to share resources, maintain context between invocations, follow object-oriented design principles, customize tools before passing them to an agent, or create different tool configurations for different agents.

### Example with Multiple Tools in a Class

You can define multiple tools within the same class to create a cohesive set of related functionality:

data-copied=&quot;Copied!&quot; data-code=&quot;class DatabaseTools { private connection: { connected: boolean; db: string } readonly queryTool: ReturnType&lt;typeof tool&gt; readonly insertTool: ReturnType&lt;typeof tool&gt; constructor(connectionString: string) { // Establish connection this.connection = { connected: true, db: &#39;example\_db&#39; } const connection = this.connection // Create query tool this.queryTool = tool({ name: &#39;query\_database&#39;, description: &#39;Run a SQL query against the database&#39;, inputSchema: z.object({ sql: z.string().describe(&#39;The SQL query to execute&#39;), }), callback: (input) =&gt; { return { results: \`Query results for: ${input.sql}\`, connection } }, }) // Create insert tool this.insertTool = tool({ name: &#39;insert\_record&#39;, description: &#39;Insert a new record into the database&#39;, inputSchema: z.object({ table: z.string().describe(&#39;The table name&#39;), data: z.record(z.string(), z.any()).describe(&#39;The data to insert&#39;), }), callback: (input) =&gt; { return \`Inserted data into ${input.table}: ${JSON.stringify(input.data)}\` }, }) }}// Usageasync function useDatabaseTools() { const dbTools = new DatabaseTools(&#39;example\_connection\_string&#39;) const agent = new Agent({ tools: \[dbTools.queryTool, dbTools.insertTool\], })}&quot;&gt;&lt;div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/button&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/figure&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;p&gt;In TypeScript, you can create tools within a class and store them as properties. The tools can access the class’s private state through closures.&lt;/p&gt; </starlight-tab-item>

## Tool Response Format

Tools can return responses in various formats using the [<code dir="auto">ToolResult</code>](/docs/api/python/strands.types.tools#ToolResult) structure. This structure provides flexibility for returning different types of content while maintaining a consistent interface.

#### ToolResult Structure

<starlight-tab-item data-label="Python"> &lt;p&gt;The &lt;a href=&quot;/docs/api/python/strands.types.tools/#ToolResult&quot;&gt;&amp;lt;code dir=&amp;quot;auto&amp;quot;&amp;gt;ToolResult&amp;lt;/code&amp;gt;&lt;/a&gt; dictionary has the following structure:&lt;/p&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;expressive-code&quot;&gt;&lt;figure class=&quot;frame&quot;&gt;&lt;figcaption class=&quot;header&quot;&gt;&lt;/figcaption&gt;&lt;pre data-language=&quot;python&quot; dir=&quot;ltr&quot;&gt;&lt;code&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;ec-line&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;code&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#24292E;--1:#E1E4E8&quot;&gt;{&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;ec-line&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;code&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;indent&quot;&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#032F62;--1:#9ECBFF&quot;&gt;&amp;quot;toolUseId&amp;quot;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#24292E;--1:#E1E4E8&quot;&gt;: &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#005CC5;--1:#79B8FF&quot;&gt;str&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#24292E;--1:#E1E4E8&quot;&gt;, &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#616972;--1:#99A0A6&quot;&gt;# The ID of the tool use request (should match the incoming request). Optional&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;ec-line&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;code&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;indent&quot;&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#032F62;--1:#9ECBFF&quot;&gt;&amp;quot;status&amp;quot;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#24292E;--1:#E1E4E8&quot;&gt;: &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#005CC5;--1:#79B8FF&quot;&gt;str&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#24292E;--1:#E1E4E8&quot;&gt;, &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#616972;--1:#99A0A6&quot;&gt;# Either &amp;quot;success&amp;quot; or &amp;quot;error&amp;quot;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;ec-line&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;code&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;indent&quot;&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#032F62;--1:#9ECBFF&quot;&gt;&amp;quot;content&amp;quot;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#24292E;--1:#E1E4E8&quot;&gt;: List\[&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#005CC5;--1:#79B8FF&quot;&gt;dict&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#24292E;--1:#E1E4E8&quot;&gt;\] &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#616972;--1:#99A0A6&quot;&gt;# A list of content items with different possible formats&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;ec-line&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;code&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#24292E;--1:#E1E4E8&quot;&gt;}&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/code&gt;&lt;/pre&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;copy&quot;&gt;&lt;div aria-live=&quot;polite&quot;&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;button title=&quot;Copy to clipboard&quot; data-copied=&quot;Copied!&quot; data-code=&quot;{ &amp;#34;toolUseId&amp;#34;: str, # The ID of the tool use request (should match the incoming request). Optional &amp;#34;status&amp;#34;: str, # Either &amp;#34;success&amp;#34; or &amp;#34;error&amp;#34; &amp;#34;content&amp;#34;: List\[dict\] # A list of content items with different possible formats}&quot;&gt;&lt;div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/button&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/figure&gt;&lt;/div&gt; data-copied=&quot;Copied!&quot; data-code=&quot;{ type: &#39;toolResultBlock&#39; toolUseId: string status: &#39;success&#39; | &#39;error&#39; content: Array&lt;ToolResultContent&gt; error?: Error}&quot;&gt;&lt;div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/button&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/figure&gt;&lt;/div&gt; </starlight-tab-item>

#### Content Types

The `content` field is a list of content blocks, where each block can contain:

-   `text`: A string containing text output
-   `json`: Any JSON-serializable data structure

</starlight-tab-item>

#### Tool Result Handling

<starlight-tab-item data-label="Python"> &lt;p&gt;When using the &lt;a href=&quot;/docs/api/python/strands.tools.decorator/#tool&quot;&gt;&amp;lt;code dir=&amp;quot;auto&amp;quot;&amp;gt;@tool&amp;lt;/code&amp;gt;&lt;/a&gt; decorator, your function’s return value is automatically converted to a proper &lt;a href=&quot;/docs/api/python/strands.types.tools/#ToolResult&quot;&gt;&amp;lt;code dir=&amp;quot;auto&amp;quot;&amp;gt;ToolResult&amp;lt;/code&amp;gt;&lt;/a&gt;:&lt;/p&gt;&lt;ol&gt; &lt;li&gt;If you return a string or other simple value, it’s wrapped as &lt;code dir=&quot;auto&quot;&gt;{&amp;quot;text&amp;quot;: str(result)}&lt;/code&gt;&lt;/li&gt; &lt;li&gt;If you return a dictionary with the proper &lt;a href=&quot;/docs/api/python/strands.types.tools/#ToolResult&quot;&gt;&amp;lt;code dir=&amp;quot;auto&amp;quot;&amp;gt;ToolResult&amp;lt;/code&amp;gt;&lt;/a&gt; structure, it’s used directly&lt;/li&gt; &lt;li&gt;If an exception occurs, it’s converted to an error response&lt;/li&gt; &lt;/ol&gt; </starlight-tab-item><starlight-tab-item data-label="TypeScript"> &lt;p&gt;The &lt;code dir=&quot;auto&quot;&gt;tool()&lt;/code&gt; function automatically handles return value conversion:&lt;/p&gt;&lt;ol&gt; &lt;li&gt;Any of the following types are converted to a ToolResult schema: &lt;code dir=&quot;auto&quot;&gt;string | number | boolean | null | { \[key: string\]: JSONValue } | JSONValue\[\]&lt;/code&gt;&lt;/li&gt; &lt;li&gt;Exceptions are caught and converted to error responses&lt;/li&gt; &lt;/ol&gt; </starlight-tab-item>

## Module Based Tools (python only)

<starlight-tab-item data-label="Python"> &lt;p&gt;An alternative approach is to define a tool as a Python module with a specific structure. This enables creating tools that don’t depend on the SDK directly.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;A Python module tool requires two key components:&lt;/p&gt;&lt;ol&gt; &lt;li&gt;A &lt;code dir=&quot;auto&quot;&gt;TOOL\_SPEC&lt;/code&gt; variable that defines the tool’s name, description, and input schema&lt;/li&gt; &lt;li&gt;A function with the same name as specified in the tool spec that implements the tool’s functionality&lt;/li&gt; &lt;/ol&gt; </starlight-tab-item>

### Basic Example

<starlight-tab-item data-label="Python"> &lt;p&gt;Here’s how you would implement the same weather forecast tool as a module:&lt;/p&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;expressive-code&quot;&gt;&lt;figure class=&quot;frame has-title&quot;&gt;&lt;figcaption class=&quot;header&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;title&quot;&gt;weather\_forecast.py&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/figcaption&gt;&lt;pre data-language=&quot;python&quot; dir=&quot;ltr&quot;&gt;&lt;code&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;ec-line&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;code&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#BF3441;--1:#F97583&quot;&gt;from&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#24292E;--1:#E1E4E8&quot;&gt; typing &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#BF3441;--1:#F97583&quot;&gt;import&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#24292E;--1:#E1E4E8&quot;&gt; Any&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;ec-line&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;code&quot;&gt; &lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;ec-line&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;code&quot;&gt; &lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;ec-line&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;code&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#616972;--1:#99A0A6&quot;&gt;# 1. ### Loading Module Tools

### Async Invocation

<starlight-tab-item data-label="Python"> &lt;p&gt;Similar to decorated tools, users may define their module tools async.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;expressive-code&quot;&gt;&lt;figure class=&quot;frame&quot;&gt;&lt;figcaption class=&quot;header&quot;&gt;&lt;/figcaption&gt;&lt;pre data-language=&quot;python&quot; dir=&quot;ltr&quot;&gt;&lt;code&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;ec-line&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;code&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#005CC5;--1:#79B8FF&quot;&gt;TOOL\_SPEC&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#24292E;--1:#E1E4E8&quot;&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#BF3441;--1:#F97583&quot;&gt;=&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#24292E;--1:#E1E4E8&quot;&gt; {&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;ec-line&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;code&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;indent&quot;&gt;
